###########################
# German Events
###########################

add_namespace = germany

# Austrian Anschluss Completed
country_event = {
	id = germany.4
	title = germany.4.t
	desc = germany.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hitler_parade
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = germany.4.a
		4 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = AUS }
				add_core_of = GER
			}
		}
		152 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = AUS }
				add_core_of = GER
			}
		}
		153 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = AUS }
				add_core_of = GER
			}
		}
		897 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = AUS }
				add_core_of = GER
			}
		}
		910 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = AUS }
				add_core_of = GER
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				153 = { is_owned_by = AUS }
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = AUS
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #Tyrol
				153 = { is_owned_by = ITA }
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = AUS
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			ITA = { transfer_state = 153 }	
			add_state_claim = 153
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #Carinthia-Styria
				897 = { is_owned_by = ITA }
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = AUS
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			ITA = { transfer_state = 897 }	
			add_state_claim = 897
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #Salzburg
				910 = { is_owned_by = ITA }
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = AUS
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			ITA = { transfer_state = 910 }	
			add_state_claim = 910
		}
		add_political_power = 75
		add_named_threat = {
			threat = 2
			name = germany.4.t
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_annexed
		set_country_flag = recent_major_land_acquisition
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Death or Dishonor"
			}
			country_event = {
				id = DOD_yugoslavia.30
				days = 4
			}
		}
		news_event = { hours = 6 id = news.36 }
	}
}
# anti_comintern_pact
# nations are asked to join pact, agreeing = relations with GER and hit with SOV 
country_event = {
	id = germany.5
	title = germany.5.t
	desc = germany.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_europe_pact

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = germany.5.a		#join
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = {
					target = SOV
					value < -10
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = GER
					value < -10
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = anti_comintern_member
		GER = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = anti_comintern_pact_opinion } }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = anti_comintern_pact_opinion }
		SOV  = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = pact_against_us } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = germany.5.b		#refuse
		trigger = { NOT = { is_puppet_of = GER } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		GER =  { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = refused_anti_comintern_pact_opinion } }
	}

}
# tripartite_pact
# anti_comintern_pact nations are asked to join pact, agreeing = relations with GER and hit with SOV
country_event = {
	id = germany.6
	title = germany.6.t
	desc = germany.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hitler_croatia_handshake
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = germany.6.a		#join
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = anti_comintern_pact_opinion }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = tripartite_pact_opinion }
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = pact_against_us }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = worse_pact_against_us }
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.6.b		#refuse
		trigger = { NOT = { is_puppet_of = GER } }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = refused_tripartite_pact_opinion }
	}
}
# molotov_ribbentrop_pact
# fire event to SOV to accept or not. adds claims
# SOV events sends reply to GER, adds claims if they said yes, hurts relations if they say no

# Molotov-Ribbentrop Pact (Soviets)
country_event = {
	id = germany.11
	title = germany.11.t
	desc = germany.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_molotov_ribentrop_handshake
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = germany.11.a	#sounds good
		
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 90 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				GER = {
					OR = { 
						has_wargoal_against = SOV
						is_justifying_wargoal_against = SOV
					}
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = {
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CZE }
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = MR_pact }# pact		
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = germany.11.a.tt
			
			add_state_claim = 96
			add_state_claim = 11
			add_state_claim = 12
			add_state_claim = 13
			add_state_claim = 190
			add_state_claim = 191
			add_state_claim = 146
			add_state_claim = 147
			add_state_claim = 722
			add_state_claim = 189
			add_state_claim = 78
			add_state_claim = 89
			add_state_claim = 91
			add_state_claim = 93
			add_state_claim = 94
			add_state_claim = 95
			add_state_claim = 96
			add_state_claim = 97
			add_state_claim = 80
			add_state_claim = 840
		
			
			hidden_effect =  {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = SOV_molotov_ribbentrop_pact days = 650
				}
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = { days = 1 id = germany.12 }
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = MR_pact }# pact
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = sov_yes_pact
		}
		
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				GER = { 
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
					NOT = { 
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = HUN		
							HUN = {
								has_completed_focus = HUN_claim_galicia
							}
						}
						has_country_flag = ah_ger_poland_pact
						}
					}
				}
			GER = { country_event = germany.321 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = HUN		
							HUN = {
								has_completed_focus = HUN_claim_galicia
							}
						}
						has_country_flag = ah_ger_poland_pact
					}				
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = germany.361 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = germany.11.b	#no way 
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				GER = {
					NOT = { has_wargoal_against = SOV }
					NOT = { is_justifying_wargoal_against = SOV }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50	
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = refused_MR_pact }# no pact 
		GER = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = germany.13 }
		}
		set_global_flag = sov_no_pact
	}
}

#GER offers Krakow

	id = germany.329
	title = germany.329.t
	desc = germany.329.desc

		GER = { country_event = germany.332 }
		set_country_flag = MR_pact_CZE_concession
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.329.b	#Not enough, leave!
		GER = { country_event = germany.331 }
		GER = { remove_from_faction = CZE }
		clr_country_flag = in_axis
	}
}

	}
}

#How to handle Sud Question - CZE
country_event = {
	id = germany.348
	title = germany.348.t
	desc = germany.348.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_politician_speech
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Demand Sudetenland
		name = germany.348.a
		ai_chance = { base = 90 } 
		trigger = {  }
			
			if =  {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ENG = { exists = no }
						ENG = {
							is_subject = yes
						}
						has_war_with = ENG
						has_war_with = FRA
						AND = {
							CZE = { is_subject = yes }
							OR = {
								CZE = { 
									NOT = {
										is_puppet_of = HUN
									}
								}
								NOT = { has_dlc = "Death or Dishonor" }
							}
						}
						CZE = { has_war_with = ENG }
						CZE = { has_war_with = FRA }
						CZE = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					}
					CZE = { controls_state = 69 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						CZE = { is_subject = no }
					}
					CZE = {
						country_event = { id = germany.122 }
					}
					else = {
						CZE = {
							OVERLORD = { country_event = { id = germany.122 } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_dlc = "Death or Dishonor"
			#		CZE = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } } #in case AH is in faction with GER and dragged a subject CZE along.
			#		OR = {
			#			69 = { is_owned_by = HUN } #AH restored
			#			AND = {
			#				CZE = { is_subject_of = HUN }
			#				69 = { is_owned_by = CZE }
			#			}
			#		}
			#	}
			#	HUN = {
			#		country_event = germany.122
			#	}
			#}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = { exists = yes }
					ENG = { is_subject = no }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ENG }
					NOT = { has_war_with = FRA }
					CZE = { is_subject = no }
					CZE = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
					CZE = { NOT = { has_war_with = ENG } }
					CZE = { controls_state = 69 }
					OR = {
						HUN = {
							NOT = {
								has_completed_focus = HUN_protect_czechoslovakia #DOD only
							}
						}
						CZE = {
							has_country_flag = HUN_AH_CZE_refused
						}
					}
				}
				ENG = {
					country_event = germany.40
				}
				add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = GER_demand_sudetenland_threat }
			}
			69 = {
				add_claim_by = GER
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { CZE = { controls_state = 69 } }
					NOT = {
						69 = { is_controlled_by = HUN }
						HUN = { has_completed_focus = HUN_protect_czechoslovakia }
					}
					69 = {
						controller = {
							NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
						}
					}
				}
				add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = GER_demand_sudetenland_threat }
				69 = {
					controller = {
						GER = {
							create_wargoal = {
								type = take_state_focus
								target = PREV
								generator = { 69 74 960 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	option = { #Prepare for Invasion
		name = germany.348.b	
		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_state_focus
			target = CZE
			generator = { 69 74 960 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5 # from 0, from 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Bring CZE closer
		name = germany.348.c
			CZE = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = ger_cze_diplomatic_focus }
				if = {
					limit = {
						GER = {
							has_government = fascism
						}
					}
					add_ideas = fascist_influence
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GER = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
					add_ideas = communist_influence
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GER = {
							has_government = monarchism
						}
					}
					add_ideas = monarchist_influence
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GER = {
							OR = {
							has_government = conservatism
							has_government = socialism
							has_government = liberalism
							}
						}
					}
					add_ideas = democratic_influence
				}
				country_event = { id = generic.1 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { hours = 6 id = news.200 }
			}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5 # from 0, from 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

### Munich Conference - CZE

# Britain
country_event = {
	id = germany.40
	title = germany.40.t
	desc = {
		text = germany.40.d
		trigger = { NOT = { has_war_with = GER } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = germany.40.d_2
		trigger = { has_war_with = GER }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_politician_speech
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Abandon the Czechs
		name = germany.40.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_4
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_6
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_7
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1 
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_8
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_9
				}
			}
		} #from 100, from 99
		trigger = { NOT = { has_war_with = GER } }
		FRA = { country_event = germany.41 }
		CZE = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = western_betrayal }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CZE = { is_guaranteed_by = ENG }
			}
			ENG = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
   					country = CZE
   					relation = guarantee
   					active = no
  				}
  				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "CZE"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Support the Czechs
		name = germany.40.b	
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10 # from 0, from 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1 
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_4
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_6
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_7
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 9 
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_8
					has_global_flag = allied_anger_9
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			remove_from_faction = GER
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			GER = { remove_from_faction = ENG }
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = condemn_aggression }
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE
					generator = { 69 74 960 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { CZE = { is_in_faction = no } }
			add_to_faction = CZE
			CZE = { set_country_flag = in_allies }
		}
		CZE = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "ENG"
				value = 200000
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				FRA = { 
					NOT = { has_war_with = CZE } 
				} 
			}
			FRA = { country_event = germany.42 }
		}
		CZE = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = offered_support }
		}
	}
}
# France (Britain Backs Down)
country_event = {
	id = germany.41
	title = germany.40.t
	desc = germany.41.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_PM_chamberlain

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Follow Britain's lead
		name = germany.41.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = CZE
			}
		}
		CZE = { 
			country_event = germany.46
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = western_betrayal }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CZE
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CZE
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = FRA
			}
			}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CZE = { is_guaranteed_by = FRA }
			}
			FRA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
   					country = CZE
   					relation = guarantee
   					active = no
  				}
  				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "CZE"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Support the Czechs alone
		name = germany.41.b	
		trigger = { is_puppet = no }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CZE
				has_completed_focus = FRA_little_entente
			}
			add_political_power = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_little_entente }
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CZE } 
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -200
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = condemn_aggression }
		CZE = { 
			country_event = germany.45
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = offered_support }
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = germany.48
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE
					generator = { 69 74 960 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			ENG = { 
				country_event = germany.43 
				remove_from_faction = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			GER = { 
				remove_from_faction = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CZE }
				CZE = { is_in_faction = no }
			}
			add_to_faction = CZE
			CZE = { set_country_flag = in_little_entente }
			CZE = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "FRA"
					value = 200000
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction = no
					is_faction_leader = no
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CZE }
				CZE = { is_in_faction = no }
			}
			set_country_flag = in_little_entente
			create_faction = "french_alliance"
			set_rule = { can_create_factions = yes }
			add_to_faction = CZE
			CZE = {
				set_country_flag = in_little_entente
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "FRA"
					value = 200000
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CZE }
				CZE = { is_in_faction = yes }
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = take_state_focus
				target = GER
				generator = { 42 895 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction = no
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
				CZE = { 
					is_in_faction = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { CZE = { has_country_flag = in_little_entente } }
			set_country_flag = in_little_entente
			}
			CZE = { add_to_faction = FRA }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "CZE"
				value = 200000
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_little_entente } }
			add_national_unity = 0.05
		}
	}
}

# France (Britain Supports the Czechs)
country_event = {
	id = germany.42
	title = germany.40.t
	desc = germany.42.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_panzer35
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Support
	option = {
		name = germany.42.a
		trigger = {
			is_puppet = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CZE }
			}
			remove_from_faction = FRA
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG } 
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CZE }
				}
			ENG = { add_to_faction = FRA }
			FRA = { set_country_flag = in_allies }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "ENG"
				value = 200000
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
					has_completed_focus = FRA_little_entente
					is_faction_leader = yes
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				}
				add_to_faction = ENG #Britain joins the little entente
				ENG = { set_country_flag = in_little_entente }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = condemn_aggression }
		CZE = { 
			country_event = germany.44
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = offered_support }
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = germany.47
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE
					generator = { 69 74 960 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Abandon
	option = {
		name = germany.42.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG has_country_flag = in_allies }
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CZE }
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10 
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = GER_has_started_war
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } #FRA doesn't care if in faction
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CZE = { is_guaranteed_by = FRA }
			}
			FRA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
   					country = CZE
   					relation = guarantee
   					active = no
  				}
  				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "CZE"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		CZE = {
			country_event = germany.44
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = western_betrayal }
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = germany.47
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE
					generator = { 69 74 960 }
				}
			}
		}		
	}
}

# Czechoslovakia (Abandoned)
country_event = {
	id = germany.46
	title = germany.46.t
	desc = germany.46.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_czech_soldiers_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Surrender the Sudetenland
		name = germany.46.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = { # Decrease chance CZE resists if AUS isn't taken first
				AUS = { exists = yes }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = { # If they stand a chance they will fight
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio > 0.75
				}
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						NOT = { tag = GER }
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #if you lead a faction, fight
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05 #if you are in a faction, maybe fight
				is_faction_leader = no
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_puppet = yes
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = GER } #puppeted CZE wouldn't surrender Sudetenland otherwise
			}
			modifier = { # Increase it again if other bordering nations are in Axis
				any_neighbor_country = {
					NOT = { tag = GER }
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				factor = 2.0
			}
		}
		GER = { country_event = germany.50 }
	}
	option = { # Refuse anyway
		name = germany.46.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = ignore
			id = "ENG"
			value = 2000
		}
		ENG = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = ignore
				id = "CZE"
				value = 20000
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = ignore
				id = "CZE"
				value = 20000
			}
		}
		GER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = GER_demand_sudetenland_rejected }
			set_global_flag = CZE_refused_sudetenland
			country_event = germany.49
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						CZE = {
							OR = { 
								is_in_faction_with = GER 
								has_country_flag = in_axis
							 }
						}
					}

					CZE = { clr_country_flag = in_axis }
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE

						has_war_with = ENG
						has_war_with = FRA

					HUN = { owns_state = 69 }
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = HUN
					generator = { 69 74 960 }
				}
			}

				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GER = {
							has_government = communism
						}

# France (Britain Backs Down)
country_event = {
	id = germany.351
	title = germany.350.t
	desc = germany.351.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_PM_chamberlain

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Follow Britain's lead
		name = germany.351.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
			}
		}
		HUN = { 
			country_event = germany.356
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = western_betrayal }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = FRA
			}
			}
	if = {
			limit = {
				HUN = { is_guaranteed_by = FRA }
			}
			FRA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
   					country = HUN
   					relation = guarantee
   					active = no
  				}
  				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "HUN"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Support the Austro-Hungarians alone
		name = germany.351.b	
		trigger = { is_puppet = no }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = HUN
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
				has_completed_focus = FRA_little_entente
			}
			add_political_power = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_little_entente }
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN } 
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -200
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = condemn_aggression }
		HUN = { 
			country_event = germany.355
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = offered_support }
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = germany.358
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = HUN
					generator = { 69 74 960 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			ENG = { 
				country_event = germany.353 
				remove_from_faction = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			GER = { 
				remove_from_faction = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }
				HUN = { is_in_faction = no }
			}
			add_to_faction = HUN
			HUN = { set_country_flag = in_little_entente }
			HUN = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "FRA"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction = no
					is_faction_leader = no
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }
				HUN = { is_in_faction = no }
			}
			set_country_flag = in_little_entente
			create_faction = "french_alliance"
			set_rule = { can_create_factions = yes }
			add_to_faction = HUN
			HUN = {
				set_country_flag = in_little_entente
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "FRA"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_little_entente } }
			add_national_unity = 0.05
		}
	}
}

# France (Britain Supports the Austro-Hungarians)
country_event = {
	id = germany.352
	title = germany.350.t
	desc = germany.352.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_panzer35
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Support
	option = {
		name = germany.352.a
	trigger = {
			is_puppet = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }
			}
			remove_from_faction = FRA
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG } 
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }
				}
			ENG = { add_to_faction = FRA }
			FRA = { set_country_flag = in_allies }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "ENG"
				value = 200000
			}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
				has_completed_focus = FRA_little_entente
				is_faction_leader = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			}
			add_to_faction = ENG #Britain joins the little entente
			ENG = { set_country_flag = in_little_entente }
		}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = condemn_aggression }
		HUN = { 
			country_event = germany.354
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = offered_support }
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = germany.357
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = HUN
					generator = { 69 74 960 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Abandon
	option = {
		name = germany.352.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG has_country_flag = in_allies }
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10 
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = GER_has_started_war
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } #FRA doesn't care if in faction
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				HUN = { is_guaranteed_by = FRA }
			}
			FRA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
   					country = HUN
   					relation = guarantee
   					active = no
  				}
  				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "HUN"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		HUN = {
			country_event = germany.44
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = western_betrayal }
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = germany.47
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = HUN
					generator = { 69 74 960 }
				}
			}
		}		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = germany.356
	title = germany.356.t
	desc = germany.356.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_czech_soldiers_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Surrender the Sudetenland
		name = germany.356.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = { # Decrease chance HUN resists if AUS isn't already taken
				AUS = { exists = yes }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = { # If they stand a chance they will fight
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio > 0.75
				}
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						NOT = { tag = GER }
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #if you lead a faction, fight
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05 #if you are in a faction, maybe fight
				is_faction_leader = no
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_puppet = yes
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = GER } #puppeted HUN wouldn't surrender Sudetenland otherwise
			}
			modifier = { # Increase it again if other bordering nations are in Axis
				any_neighbor_country = {
					NOT = { tag = GER }
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				factor = 2.0
			}
		}
		GER = { country_event = germany.360 }
	}
	option = { # Refuse anyway
		name = germany.356.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		GER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = GER_demand_sudetenland_rejected }
			set_global_flag = CZE_refused_sudetenland
			country_event = germany.359
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						HUN = {
							OR = { 
								is_in_faction_with = GER 
								has_country_flag = in_axis
							 }
						}
					}		
					GER = { remove_from_faction = HUN }
					HUN = { clr_country_flag = in_axis }
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = HUN
					generator = { 69 74 960 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# French Response
country_event = {
	id = germany.60
	title = germany.60.t
	desc = germany.60.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_troops
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # This means war!
		name = germany.60.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 1 
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio > 0.7
				}
				NOT = { has_idea = FRA_disjointed_government }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -150
		add_national_unity = -0.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				ENG = {
					is_puppet = no
					NOT = { has_war_with = FRA }
				}
			}
			ENG = {
				country_event = germany.61
				custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
				effect_tooltip = { add_to_faction = FRA FRA = { set_country_flag = in_allies } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FRA_disjointed_government
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = germany.60.a.tt
			effect_tooltip = {
				#start_civil_war = {

	id = germany.61
	title = germany.60.t
	desc = germany.61.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_british_inspect_troops
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # War out of the question
		name = germany.61.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		FRA = { 
			country_event = { hours = 6 id = germany.63 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Support France
		name = germany.61.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio > 0.7
				}
			} 
		}
		add_political_power = -150
		add_national_unity = -0.2
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = FRA NOT = { has_war_with = ENG } }
				ENG = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				FRA = { set_country_flag = in_allies }
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "ENG"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FRA = { is_in_faction = no } }
			add_to_faction = FRA
			FRA = {
				set_country_flag = in_allies
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "ENG"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		FRA = { 
			country_event = { hours = 6 id = germany.64 }
		}
	}
}

### Oster Conspiracy
# Conspiracy Begins!
country_event = {
	id = germany.70
	title = germany.70.t
	desc = germany.70.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_germans_in_sudentenland_1938
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = { name = "Adolf Hitler" }
		tag = GER
		AND = {
			CZE = { has_capitulated = no }
			country_exists = CZE # Should only trigger if CZE hasn't fallen
		}
		has_war_with = CZE
		has_war_with = FRA
		has_war_with = ENG
		has_country_flag = allies_support_czechs
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 150
	}
	
	option = {
		name = germany.70.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { any_war_score < 39 } }
				random_list = {
					20 = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = germany.71 } } # Conspiracy defeated, but Hitler dead
					75 = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = germany.72 } } # Conspiracy defeated, Hitler survives
					5 = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = germany.73 } } # Conspiracy successful, Civil War
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { any_war_score < 39 }
				random_list = {
					33 = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = germany.71 } } # Conspiracy defeated, but Hitler dead
					33 = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = germany.72 } } # Conspiracy defeated, Hitler survives
					33 = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = germany.73 } } # Conspiracy successful, Civil War
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# A Solution for Danzig
country_event = {
	id = germany.340
	title = germany.340.t
	desc = germany.340.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_polish_border

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Danzig or War
		name = germany.340.a
		add_named_threat = { threat = 5 name = GER_danzig_or_war }
			if = {
				limit = {
					85 = {
						controller = {
							tag = POL
							has_civil_war = no
						}
					}
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					transfer_state = 85
					remove_state_claim = 86
				}
				POL = {
					country_event = { id = germany.86 }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT } }
						custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT 
							ROOT = { is_faction_leader = yes }
						}
						custom_effect_tooltip = GER_danzig_or_war_POL_faction_GER_leader
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT 
							NOT = { ROOT = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
						}
						custom_effect_tooltip = GER_danzig_or_war_POL_faction_GER_noleader
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					85 = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								original_tag = POL
								tag = POL
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = POL
						has_civil_war = yes
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							has_volunteers_amount_from = {
								tag = GER
								count > 0
							}
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = germany.113 days = 1 }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_danzig_or_war_POL_civil_war
			}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75	
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Offer Slovakia for Danzig
		name = germany.340.b
		trigger = {
			is_puppet = no
			OR = {
				SLO = {
					exists = yes
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				owns_state = 70
			}
			NOT = { owns_state = 85 }
			NOT = { has_war_with = POL }
			POL = { owns_state = 72 }
		}
		POL = {
			country_event = { id = germany.80 days = 1 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}			
		}		
		
	}
	
	option = { #Influence/Ally Them
		name = germany.340.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = sov_yes_pact }
			NOT = { has_war_with = POL }
		}
		POL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = ger_pol_diplomacy_focus }
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				add_ideas = fascist_influence
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				add_ideas = communist_influence
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						democratic_govt = yes
					}
				}
				add_ideas = democratic_influence
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						has_government = monarchism
					}
				}
				add_ideas = monarchist_influence
			}

			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes

country_event = {

	desc = germany.80.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_polish_border

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = germany.80.a
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			
		}

		GER = { country_event = { id = germany.81 days = 1 } }
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { SLO = { exists = yes } }
				annex_country = { target = SLO }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { owns_state = 70 } }
				transfer_state = 70
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { owns_state = 71 } }
				transfer_state = 71
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { owns_state = 73 } }
				transfer_state = 73
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { owns_state = 664 } }
				transfer_state = 664
			}
			GER = { transfer_state = 85 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {	
		name = germany.80.b
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}			
		}		
		GER = {
			country_event = { id = germany.82 days = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					is_in_faction_with = POL
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = POL
				POL = { clr_country_flag = in_axis }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					is_in_faction_with = POL
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = { 
						is_in_faction_with = GER
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					remove_from_faction = GER
				}
			}				
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = POL
					generator = { 85 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poland Accepts, Cedes Danzig
country_event = {
	id = germany.81
	title = germany.81.t
	desc = germany.81.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_polish_border

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = germany.81.a
		set_country_flag = peaceful_danzig
		if = {
			limit = { SLO = { exists = yes } }
			POL = { annex_country = { target = SLO } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 70 }
			POL = { transfer_state = 70 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 71 }
			POL = { transfer_state = 71 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 73 }
			POL = { transfer_state = 73 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 664 }
			POL = { transfer_state = 664 }
		}
		transfer_state = 85
		set_country_flag = recent_major_land_acquisition
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { hours= 6 id = news.202 }
			set_global_flag = poland_swap_danzig
		}
	}
}

#sov-ger unholy alliance 
country_event = {
	id = germany.89
	title = germany.89.t
	desc = germany.89.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_molotov_ribbentrop_pact

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = germany.89.a
		dismantle_faction = yes
		add_national_unity = -0.1
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { tag = GER }
						has_government = fascism 
					}
					OR = {
					#has_government = conservatism
					has_government = conservatism
					has_government = liberalism
					has_government = socialism
					} 
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = unholy_alliance }
		}
		GER = {
			if = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction  = yes
					}
					remove_from_faction = GER
			}
			set_country_flag = in_berlin_moscow_axis
			add_national_unity = -0.2
			create_faction = "the_berlin_moscow_axis"
			add_to_faction = SOV
			SOV = { set_country_flag = in_berlin_moscow_axis }
			add_named_threat = { threat = 5 name = germany.89.t }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = GER }
					has_government = fascism 
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = communist_collaborators }
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
					#has_government = conservatism
					has_government = conservatism
					has_government = liberalism
					has_government = socialism
					} 
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = unholy_alliance }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			# Britain can rally democracies
			ENG = {
				country_event = { days = 3 id = britain.11 }
			}
			# US drops communism/fascism
			USA = {
				country_event = { id = usa.14 }
				country_event = { id = usa.24 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = germany.89.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		GER = {
			country_event = germany.90
			effect_tooltip = {
				remove_ideas = soviet_german_friendship
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = SOV
					generator = { 219 217 } # Moscow and Stalingrad
				}
			}
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = ger_sov_alliance_focus }
		remove_ideas = soviet_german_friendship
	}
}

					}

			}

			add_named_threat = { threat = 5 name = GER_fate_of_yugoslavia }
			CRO = {
				transfer_state = 103
				transfer_state = 104

				transfer_state = 902

					transfer_state = 907
					transfer_state = 108
					transfer_state = 107
					transfer_state = 906
			}

					transfer_state = 914
					transfer_state = 45
				}

					transfer_state = 106
					transfer_state = 905
				}

					transfer_state = 913
					transfer_state = 916

						}

						transfer_state = 105
						transfer_state = 904
						transfer_state = 903
					}

# Germany: Carve up Greece - Take land for Germany?
country_event = {
	id = germany.101
	title = germany.101.t
	desc = germany.101.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_german_inspect_troops
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				731 = {
					any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = GER }
					is_owned_by = GRE
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = GER_second_ljubljana_award_GER_731
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				185 = {
					any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = GER }
					is_owned_by = GRE
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = GER_second_ljubljana_award_GER_185
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				47 = {
					any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = GER }
					is_owned_by = GRE
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = GER_second_ljubljana_award_GER_47
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = germany.101.a
		GRE = { country_event = { id = greece.2 hours = 2 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = germany.101_tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_global_flag = GER_second_ljubljana_award_GER_731
				}
				GER = { transfer_state = 731 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_global_flag = GER_second_ljubljana_award_GER_185
					NOT = { has_global_flag = GER_second_ljubljana_award_GER_731 }
				}
				GER = { transfer_state = 185 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_global_flag = GER_second_ljubljana_award_GER_47
					NOT = { has_global_flag = GER_second_ljubljana_award_GER_731 }
					NOT = { has_global_flag = GER_second_ljubljana_award_GER_185 }
				}
				GER = { transfer_state = 47 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = germany.101.b
	}
}

	desc = { text = germany.104.d_Corsica 				trigger = { has_global_flag = ITA_claims_on_france_1 } }
	desc = { text = germany.104.d_Savoy_Corsica 	trigger = { has_global_flag = ITA_claims_on_france_735 has_global_flag = ITA_claims_on_france_1 } }
 
 
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_italian_pact

# Germany: Treaty Of Craiova
country_event = {
	id = germany.106
	title = germany.106.t
	desc = { 
		text = germany.106.d_second_vienna_accepted_all
		trigger = {
			ROM = { has_country_flag = second_vienna_accepted_all }
		}
	}
	desc = { 
		text = germany.106.d_second_vienna_accepted_north
		trigger = {
			ROM = { has_country_flag = second_vienna_accepted_north }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = germany.106.d_no_vienna
		trigger = {
			ROM = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = second_vienna_accepted_all }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = second_vienna_accepted_north }
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_vienna_award_hungary
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Give Bulgaria state 77
		name = germany.106.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 95 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				BUL = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				}
			}
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = germany.106_threat }
		BUL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = GER_treaty_of_craiova_GER }

			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					is_faction_leader = yes 
					NOT = { tag = GER }
				}				
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = BUL modifier = GER_treaty_of_craiova_other }
			}
		}
		ROM = {
			country_event = { id = romania.5 hours = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Give Bulgaria nothing
		name = germany.106.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				NOT = {
					BUL = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		BUL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = GER_treaty_of_craiova_noland }
			country_event = { id = bulgaria.5 hours = 4 }
		}
	}
}

#The Yalta Conference
country_event = {
	id = germany.118
	title = germany.118.t
	desc = germany.118.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_churchill_roosevelt_stalin_conference

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		SOV ={ has_war_with = GER }
		has_war_with = GER
		is_historical_focus_on = yes
		is_faction_leader = yes
		NOT = { has_global_flag = had_yalta_conference }
		OR = {
		AND = {
		any_state = {
			is_core_of = GER
			controller = {
				is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			}
		
		any_state = {
			is_core_of = GER
			controller = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOV }
			}
		}
		
		GER = { surrender_progress > 65 }
		}
	}

		days = 15
	}

		set_global_flag = had_yalta_conference

					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE

				}
			}
		}

			}
		}

			factor = 0
		}

		}
	}
}

#Event if Austria has a civil war
country_event = {
	id = germany.126
	title = germany.126.t
	desc = germany.126.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = germany.126.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				OR = {
					has_government = neutrality
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}

		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = AUS
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			}
			FROM = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = ROOT
					enemy = PREV
				}
				annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes }
				hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = news.237 } }
			}

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.126.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				OR = {
					has_government = communism
					has_government = conservatism
					has_government = liberalism
					has_government = socialism
					}
			}

		}

		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = AUS
					original_tag = AUS
				}

			}
			FROM = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}

			}

		}
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = germany.233
	title = germany.233.t
	desc = germany.233.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_kubelwagon_in_afrika

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = germany.233.a
		trigger = { 
			tag = GER
			is_ai = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = "GER_afrikakorps_ai"
			set_country_flag = GERafrikakorp
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.233.b
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			date > 1941.2.9
			is_ai = no
			GER = { has_tech = desert_equipment }
			GER = { has_tech = HVantiair2 }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = "GER_afrikakorps"
			set_country_flag = GERafrikakorp
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.233.c		#refuse
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
			trigger = {
			tag = GER
			date > 1941.2.9
			is_ai = no
			NOT = {GER = { has_tech = desert_equipment }}
			NOT = {GER = { has_tech = HVantiair2 }}
		}
		set_country_flag = GERafrikakorp
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = germany.258
	title = germany.258.t
	desc = { 
		text = germany.258.desc.a
		trigger = { 
			has_tech = tech_kr_bb 
			is_ai = no
		}
	}
	desc = { 
		text = germany.258.desc.b
		trigger = { 
			has_tech = tech_kr_bb_38
			is_ai = no
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_scharnhorst_28

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = no
		OR = {
			has_tech = tech_kr_bb
			has_tech = tech_kr_bb_38
			not = { has_country_flag = scharnhorst_28 }

country_event = {
	id = germany.266
	title = germany.266.t
	desc = germany.266.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Pz_I
	
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_country_flag = impossible
		has_equipment = { panzer_i_equipment > 500 }
		has_tech = subtech_light_panzer_td_equipment_1
		not = { has_country_flag = pzj_1}
		has_global_flag = end_of_czechoslovakia #uses czech AT guns
		has_country_flag = czech_equipment
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = { flag = pzj_1 days = 180 } 
	}
		
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = germany.266.a	#convert Pz 1
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }	# tanks more useful to the AI

		send_equipment = {
			target = CZE	#needs testing with CZE			
			type = panzer_i_equipment
			amount = 500
		}     
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = "GER_PanzerJaeger1"
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = germany.266.b #No need
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

#Fritsch Affair
country_event = {
	id = germany.279
	title = germany.279.t
	desc = germany.279.desc
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		date > 1937.2.1
		date < 1937.2.10
		has_government = fascist
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}

	option = { #Fire Fritsch
		name = germany.279.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_national_unity = 0.01
		remove_ideas = werner_von_fritsch
		add_ideas = adolf_hitler
		add_ideas = wilhelm_keitel
		set_country_flag = fritsch_fired
	}
	option = { #Keep Fritsch
		name = germany.279.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_national_unity = -0.05
		set_country_flag = fritsch_kept	
	}
	option = { #Fire Fritsch AI
		name = germany.279.c
		trigger = {
			is_ai = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_national_unity = 0.01
		remove_ideas = fritsch_ai
		add_ideas = adolf_hitler
		add_ideas = wilhelm_keitel_ai
		set_country_flag = fritsch_dead	
	}
}
#AI minister switch
country_event = {
	id = germany.280
	title = germany.280.t
	desc = germany.280.d

	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Get em out

# Wilhelm III dies
country_event = {
	id = germany.301
	title = germany.301.t
	desc = germany.301.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		OR = { 
			has_government = monarchism
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_government = conservatism
					has_government = socialism
					has_government = liberalism
				}
				has_country_flag = const_kaiser
			}
		}
		date > 1951.3.10
		has_country_flag = wilhelm_iii_chosen
	}
	
	immediate = { set_country_flag = wilhelm_iii_dead clr_country_flag = wilhelm_iii_chosen }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 120
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			date > 1951.6.1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = germany.301.a
		add_national_unity = -0.02
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Ferdinand I"
			desc = "Kaiser of the German Empire"
			picture = "Portrait_Germany_Louis_Ferdinand.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = imperial
			traits = {
				monarchist
				great_leader
			}
		}
	}
}
#Which Kaiser should we have?
country_event = {
	id = germany.302
	title = germany.302.t
	desc = germany.302.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		OR = { 
			has_government = monarchism
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_government = conservatism
					has_government = socialism
					has_government = liberalism
				}
				has_country_flag = const_kaiser
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = kaiser_chosen }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	immediate = { set_country_flag = kaiser_chosen }
	
	option = { #Keep Wilhelm III
		name = germany.302.a
		add_political_power = 30
		add_national_unity = -0.05
		set_country_flag = wilhelm_iii_chosen
		country_event = germany.303
	}
	option = { #Install Louis Ferdinand
		name = germany.302.b
		set_country_flag = ferdinand_chosen
		add_political_power = -30
		add_national_unity = 0.05
		retire_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Ferdinand I"
			desc = "POLITICS_LOUIS_FERDINAND_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Germany_Louis_Ferdinand.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = imperial
			traits = {
				monarchist
				great_leader
			}
		}
		country_event = germany.303
	}
}

	id = germany.303
	title = germany.303.t
	desc = germany.303.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { set_country_flag = chancellor_chosen }

	option = { #von Papen
		name = germany.303.a
		set_country_flag = papen_chosen
		add_ideas = franz_von_papen
		add_political_power = 50
		add_national_unity = -0.03
		monarchism_minus_3 = yes
		fascism_plus_2 = yes
		socialism_plus_3 = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				monarchism > 0.55
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Lettow-Vorbeck
		name = germany.303.b
		set_country_flag = lv_chosen
		add_ideas = paul_von_lettow_vorbeck
		add_political_power = 10
		add_national_unity = 0.06
		monarchism_plus_3 = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				monarchism < 0.35
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #v. Blumenthal
		name = germany.303.c
		set_country_flag = blumenthal_chosen
		add_ideas = hans_jurgen_von_blumenthal
		add_political_power = -30
		add_national_unity = 0.05
		conservatism_plus_3 = yes
		monarchism_plus_3 = yes
		socialism_plus_3 = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				monarchism < 0.55
				monarchism > 0.35
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.303.d
		set_country_flag = no_ger_chancellor
		add_political_power = 75
		add_national_unity = -0.05
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = wilhelm_iii_chosen }
			add_ideas = wilhelm_iii
		}
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = ferdinand_chosen }
			add_ideas = louis_ferdinand
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_country_flag = wilhelm_iii_chosen
				monarchism > 0.50
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = germany.315
	title = germany.315.t
	desc = germany.315.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = {  }

	option = { 
		name = germany.315.a
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = em_clean_referendum }
			random_list = {
				60 = { BEL = { country_event = germany.316 } }
				40 = { GER = { country_event = germany.317 } }
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = em_dirty_referendum }
			random_list = {
				95 = { BEL = { country_event = germany.316 } }
				5 = { GER = { country_event = germany.317 } }
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { }
				25 = { GER = { country_event = germany.318 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Allied Anger: Trigger to time how long until reduction event can fire
country_event = {
	id = germany.376
	title = germany.376.t
	desc = germany.376.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_politician_speech
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = recent_major_land_acquisition
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 90
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = allied_anger_4
				has_global_flag = allied_anger_5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = allied_anger_6
				has_global_flag = allied_anger_7
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.65
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = allied_anger_8
				has_global_flag = allied_anger_9
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = allied_anger_10
				has_war_with = ENG
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = germany.376.a	
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = ENG } }
			set_country_flag = good_boy_GER			
		}
		clr_country_flag = recent_major_land_acquisition
	}
}

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ITA = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				}
			ITA = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = GER enemy = YUG }}
		}
			if = {
				limit = {
					HUN = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				}
			HUN = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = GER enemy = YUG }}
		}
		if = {
				limit = {
					ROM = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				}
			ROM = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = GER enemy = YUG }}
		}
		if = {
				limit = {
					BUL = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				}
			BUL = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = GER enemy = YUG }}
		}
		if = {
				limit = {
					GRE = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				}
			GRE = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = GER enemy = YUG }}
		}
		}
		GER = { country_event = germany.457 }
	}
}
